## **176 - Hot Spring Resort of Dreams! (2) ~Door to paradise~**

As a matter of fact, there was a bit of a fuss at the time they entered.

It seemed that usually this was where the man and the security personnel parted ways.

And they were supposed to come and pick him up on the day he left.

It was explained that there was no opening in the facility’s security, with surveillance cameras monitoring those who entered and left and plain-clothed security guards patrolling the premise, but Kanako and Touko showed some reluctance.

That was because if they were to be informed by phone or pager that something had happened to Yuu, it would take three hours, even if they sped through the expressway, to get there.

They were probably used to security personnel worrying about being separated from the man who was visiting for the first time.

The compromise offered by Satsuki was that since they had reserved a room in the adjacent resort condominium, she asked the security personnel to stay there.

If it was from there, they would be able to rush there within 30 minutes.

Kanako and Touko agreed to it, albeit reluctantly, and decided to go to the condominium via the underground parking lot, so they parted ways there for the time being.

It was decided that once they knew the number of the room where they would be staying, they would contact him later.

After that, Yuu was shown into a small conference room that looked like it could be found in any office.

There was a rectangular table with about ten chairs.

When Yuu and the others entered, two women were sitting in two of them.

「Sorry to keep you waiting!」

「Ah, no…?!」

The one sitting on the opposite side of them showed a surprised look on her face when she saw Yuu.

The woman sitting in front of them was also stunned with her jaw dropping.

「Ufufu. First thing first, let’s have you, elder sisters and younger brother who are meeting for the first time, introduce yourself to each other. Come over here.」

As Yuu walked into the room while being led by the hand by Satsuki, the two women also jumped and got up from their seats.

Across the table, the woman on the left from Yuu’s perspective was in her early twenties. She was more than 5cm taller than Yuu and had broad shoulders, giving her a well-built figure.

She was dressed in a plain white polo shirt and tight-fitting three-quarter length jeans.

Her dark brown hair, which barely reached her back, was tied up into a single bundle, and her face, with exposed forehead, was beautifully tanned to light brown color. She was an athletic-type person who gave off a lively impression.

And yet she radiated no intimidating air and gave off a gentle impression, which was probably because she was a likeable, beautiful woman with round eyes.

In fact, once the initial shock wore off, she looked at Yuu with a friendly smile on her face.

The woman on the right didn’t seem to be that much apart from Yuu in age, and was short, probably less than 160cm tall.

Having only looked at him once, she was looking down, unable to look Yuu in the eye. And perhaps because of her hunched back, she looked a little chubby.

Since a while ago, she had been constantly playing with her long black hair and was restless.

She was wearing a ladylike outfit consisting of a loose-fitting pink with a small floral pattern and a long light blue flared skirt.

Although the two of them give off very contrasting impressions, it felt like they shared a certain similarity in appearance.

「Now then, let’s start with you two.」

「Alright. Then, I’ll go first. Nice to meet you. I’m… Mana. I’m 23 years old. I work in sales for a sports manufacturer in Yokohama. And this is my younger sister, c’mon.」

「I… I’m… Rina. T-t-t-… this year, I, I’m going to… a vo, vo, vocation! Vocational school.」

「Oh my, you’re as stiff as a board.」

「It can’t be helped, Satsuki-san. Rina has no experience with men at all, after all.」

According to them, they were sisters born to the same mother in Gifu Prefecture.

After graduating from high school in March this year, Rina went on to a voice acting school in Tokyo, and they started living together.

Hearing that, Yuu was convinced.

He thought the reason why Rina’s voice sounded childish, or rather high-pitched, was because she was nervous, but it turned out that she had the so-called anime voice.

It seemed that, even without needing to consciously make it that way, she had always had that kind of voice.

The shock from meeting someone who spoke with an anime voice in real life ended up making Yuu freeze, but as he was being stared at by those around him, he realized that it was his turn now.

「Ah, sorry. My name is Yuu. I’m in my first year of high school, and I’m 16 years old. Nice to meet you. Um, big sis Mana… is it fine if I call you that?」

「Big sis Mana… fine, totally fine! Dear me, to be able to meet a little brother who’s still in high school, big sis is so happy.」

When Yuu extended his right hand, Mana shook it firmly, though she blushed a little.

Perhaps it was due to the nature of her job, she seemed to be able to interact naturally with men.

Next, he turned his gaze to Rina.

It seemed that it was true that she had no immunity to men, because as she got stared at head on by Yuu, she appeared to be falling into panic, going 「Awawa」.

「C’mon, Rina, pull yourself together! You’ve taken the trouble to come here, after all.」

「I, I mean, big sis, for such a prince-like sparkling boy to suddenly appear… He’s too dazzling for a mob character like me, my eyes are going to go blind.」

「O, oh you, this isn’t a manga or anime.」

「Uu, unlike through the monitor, how do you interact with a boy in real life… A, are there no choices?」

「Big sis Rina.」

「Ah, yesh!」

When Yuu put his hands on the table and leaned forward to stare at her, Rina, flustered, pulled away instead.

Perhaps she had never had any opportunities to interact with men, and only ever spoke to them in so-called otome games.

She was like an otaku in Yuu’s previous world who was addicted to gal games and had no luck with women in real life.

But to Yuu, she, who was rambling on with a strangely childish voice, looked cute.

Here, I’d love to get close with her, by all means.

Thinking so, Yuu quickly walked around the table and approached Rina.

Surprised, Rina tried to back away in a panic, but Mana, who understood Yuu’s intention, held her back, so she and Yuu ended up facing each other up close.

Yuu immediately took Rina’s hand and held it tightly with both of his.

It was a girlish, small and soft hand.

Yuu peered into Rina, whose face turned bright red and looked as if it was emitting steam, and whispered.

「You’re so cute, big sis Rina.」

「Hau! Huh… c-c-c, cute?」

「Yeah, you’re older than me, but you’re cute. I want to get to know you better, so let’s get along well, big sis.」

「Ya…」

「「Wha!」」

The ones who let out a cry at the same time were Yuu and Mana.

This was because Rina’s eyes rolled back and she was about to fall.

Then again, Mana was holding her back, so she didn’t fall, though.

「I had heard about it beforehand, but I can’t believe he’s used to dealing with older women at that age. It’s just like…」

「Yeah…」

Yuu could hear some voices whispering about something, but when Rina, who had regained consciousness, raised her elbows and crossed her arms tightly, her cleavage swelled up, and seeing that, his eyes ended up getting glued to it.

According to what Rina said, albeit in a stammering manner, it seemed that having him whisper those words, which was the exact line from an otome game in which the heroine was a young girl who was adopted into a family with brothers, to her had made her brain heat up.

---

「Well then, can we get into it now?」

「Yes.」

「I, I’m sorry.」

Once Rina had calmed down, Hiromi stood at the very back of the room.

Near her sat Masaki and Satsuki, and Yuu, Mana, and Rina were sitting facing each other around the center of the table.

Rina’s face was still bright red.

T, that’s…

With the lights in the room turned off, a rounded rectangular light appeared on the screen hanging on the back wall.

In front of Hiromi, who was standing in the corner of the room, was a square device, from which an arm-like object extended upwards and broke in the middle. And the lens on the top of the device was emitting a warm white-colored light.

It was an overhead projector (OHP) that was once used for briefings and presentations but had become extinct, replaced by projector equipment that could be connected directly to a PC via a cable.

It was no longer in use at the company Yuu joined as a new graduate, and he once saw it covered in dust in the back of the storage room.

He heard that since there was no longer any opportunity to use it, it was discarded when they reorganized the storage room a few years later.

However, here in 1990 it appeared to be still in active use.

「Yusu-sama, Rina-sama. Since both of you are visiting this place for the first time, allow me to give you a general overview of Hesperis.

To begin with, Hesperis is the name of the Greek goddess of twilight, and the 『Garden of the Hesperides』, which is looked after by her daughters, is said to be the model and origin of the word paradise…」

According to her, the idea was originally conceived by the late Toyota Sakuya.

It was said that despite his busy schedule, he, who loved his family, would stay in places of scenic beauty around the country several times a year with a number of his wives and children.

However, wherever he went, he was the center of attention, and was always surrounded by press corps and curious onlookers.

Even if he himself was fine with it, they had small children, so he wanted to spend time alone with his family sometimes.

There were the villas that wealthy women had told him he could use freely, but he wanted a hideaway-like villa that no one would know about.

So, among his wife, lovers, and women he had exchanged feelings with, Sakuya asked for cooperation from those who were house builders, working for construction companies, and also bureaucrats in the Ministry of Construction.

What he had in mind was a mountain villa that could accommodate 10 to 15 people at most.

However, he thought it would be better to leave it to the experts, so after only making one instruction, that was the place had to be in Hakone, he left it entirely to them.

That was five years before Sakuya passed away.

Thus, the project to build a villa for Toyota Sakuya-sama’s esteemed family was launched.

The project members included companies that were competing for market share, and when even the directors got involved and said 「We’re going to build a villa that’s even more impressive than our rivals’!」, the scale of the project rapidly grew from the planning stage.

In the end, Sakuya was asked to choose from the three remaining proposals.

He was surprised by the scale, which far exceeded his expectations, but he couldn’t bring himself to throw away the plan that they had worked on day and night, and it was said that among the proposals he chose was one that was close to the current hot spring resort.

In terms of scale, they designed it to be able to accommodate 300 people, more than the total number of his wives, children, and lovers.

It couldn’t be denied that they had an ulterior motive of wanting to use the resort not only for Sakuya’s family but also for themselves.

It was just that, at such a scale, it was too large to be used as a secret hideaway, so they decided to also build a dummy, or rather a front facility, with the cooperation from the government.

And that was the Geothermal Energy Research and Development Corporation.

As a clean energy alternative to nuclear power, in addition to wind and solar power generation, basic research on geothermal energy had also been conducted at several universities, taking advantage of the country’s volcanic climate.

A public-private sector development facility had been built in Beppu, Oita Prefecture, but they decided to use this opportunity to build one in eastern Japan as well.

Incidentally, after it was completed, Sakuya himself used it only once with his family.

Instead, it was said to have served as a refuge for his wives and children to stay there after his death to avoid getting caught up in the chaos and media coverage.

The wives and children who stayed there following Sakuya’s death spent a long time talking about it.

In order to make use of the tangible and intangible legacies left by Sakuya and to ensure the coordination and unity of the family in the future, the Toyota Sakuya Memorial Foundation was established with the cooperation of the government. The foundation would also be primarily responsible for managing and operating the facility there.

---

Apparently, being projected by the projector was the cross-sectional diagram of the facility.

The right side of the diagram was high above ground level like a multi-floor building, while the left side was a semicircle about half that height. Instead, it stretched deep underground.

「As shown here, Hesperis as a hot spring resort is on the left side, which means the west side. The aboveground area is dome-shaped, with a botanical garden and pool that make use of the hot springs to maintain a constant temperature even in winter. The first underground floor is home to a parking lot, as well as the conference room, where we are currently in, board room, and storage room. From the second underground floor and beyond, they are equipped with various facilities for users. On the east side, from the first underground floor to the second aboveground floor are the corporation’s offices and research center, and from the third to the seventh floor are the resort condominiums. However, not even single of them is sold to the general public, and apart from the seventh floor, which is entirely reserved by the foundation, the rest is distributed to companies that have contributed in the construction and maintenance of this place.」

「Which means, when staying overnight, we stay on the seventh floor?」

「No, be it men or women, those who are here on a short stay of less than a week will have to stay in the underground rest house. The rooms on the seventh floor will be used to accommodate the long-stay groups as well as the men’s security personnel. Also, the seventh floor of the condominium is directly connected the shared parking lot on the first underground floor via an elevator.」

The parking lot was divided into east and west, and card authentication was required to access the connecting passage.

The security personnel were given guest cards in advance, so they could enter the parking lot on this side, but apparently, they had designed it so that the entrance from earlier could only be accessed by calling a regular member.

「To begin with, the purpose of this facility was to deepen the relationship and interaction between each member of the family, who have gone their separate ways since Toyota Sakuya-shi’s passing. To that end, the men can basically stay for free, and even the women can stay for a cheaper price than at a regular hotel. It’s just that, in order to maintain and operate such a large facility, we need government subsidies and financing from various companies, so we have no choice but to accept users from related parties. That’s why, of the female users, more than half are guest members.」

In terms of ratio of the number of women, regular members – such as Yuu’s step-mothers and sisters – were fewer in number, and since they were given priority, their requests to use the facility were easily granted.

On the other hand, guest members were much greater in number, but as opposed to deciding the order by lottery, they gave priority to the younger ones, which seemed to be done for the sake of the male regular members.

Yuu was relieved to hear that.

Conversely, knowing that he would be surrounded by ten times as many young women, including his half-elder sister, in this closed resort facility, made his heart flutter.

「Well then, that’s pretty much it for the overview of the facility. To maintain confidentiality, we don’t distribute any materials, so please commit them to your memory. Now then, next, I would like to ask Masaki-sama and Satsuki-sama to give us some points to note when using the facility.」

The screen showing the diagram of the facility remained as it was, but it seemed that there was a change in the person in charge of giving the explanation.

「Err, I, Satsuki, and Ma-kun… Masaki-kun are the oldest among us brothers and sisters who are staying here this week, so we will serve as the leaders. Now, applause!」

There, not only Yuu, but Mana and Rina also applauded.

「Thanks! Mana has been here many times, so I think she knows it already, but since today is Yuu and Rina’s first time here, we’re going to explain some things, so listen carefully, okay?」

「「Yes!」」

「First of all, the most important thing. That is, like in a regular hotel, food doesn’t pop out of thin air. To maintain secrecy, there are no staff members stationed in the underground area of Hesperis, except for security guards, you see. That’s why we divide all the guests into groups, and each group is in charge of cooking, laundry, and cleaning.」

「Those who have stayed there may know, but it’s like a rental villa that only provides living facilities.」

「Huh, then… We’ll also need to make tonight’s meals ourselves?」

「Ah, you’re exempt on the first day. After dinner each day, we divide everyone into groups for the next day. For better or worse, we’ll take each person’s wishes into consideration, but things won’t necessarily go as you wish, so even if you’re assigned a task you’re not good at, please do your best and cooperate with the others, okay?!」

For example, if you were assigned to the laundry group, you would have to spend the whole morning doing everyone’s laundry, which generally took about 2-3 hours.

On the other hand, it seemed that the cooking group started preparing dinner at 5pm, and they had to prepare the food for the morning as well.

Cleaning was done in the morning, and the location changed depending on the day, but it seemed like it would be a lot of work considering how large this place was.

As far as Yuu was concerned, he inwardly thought that, if possible, he would prefer to be assigned to the cooking group, which he was used to.

After that, they continued with the explanation, but they were all common-sense things such as, even though they were in the middle of a mountain, they should not go too wild and make too much noises, (women) should not fight (over men), and they should take good care of the facility’s belongings.

Yuu was told that if there were any women who were persistently hitting on him, the leaders would deal with it.

Since today was his first day there, it seemed that tonight, Satsuki, Mana, and Rina would be tasked with guarding him until he went to sleep.

Being assigned this important task, Mana looked extremely happy, and Rina, although embarrassed, also seemed to be unable to hide her joy.

As far as Yuu was concerned, he would love to have the three of them come up to his bed as they were, but he thought he would wait and see how things developed for now and refrain from saying anything unnecessary, but…

「Before we end it, let me confirm just one thing with Yuu.」

Once they were done with the explanation, generally with Satsuki taking the lead and Masaki providing supplementary information every now and then, the two of them stared intently at Yuu, so he instinctively put himself on guard.

「No, there’s no need to be so on guard. We’ve heard about you to some extent from Hiromi-san over there, so we just want to make sure.」

Masaki smiled.

He was so good-looking that Yuu couldn’t help but think: If I were a woman, I probably would’ve ended up getting captivated by him.

The destructive power of the smile of a handsome man or beautiful woman was off the chart.

Also, he was a little curious about what he meant by 「We’ve heard about you from Hiromi-san.」

「Of everyone here now, you’re the youngest, a high school boy, so I think you’ll be very popular. Most likely ten, no, more than twenty women would ask to have sexual relations with you. Are you prepared to choose a few from among them and spend the night with them?」

So that’s the case.

Yuu muttered to himself inwardly.

That was exactly what Yuu wished for.

Yuu got up from his seat.

「Well, I also have my own preferences, so I can’t say that I’m fine with anyone, but… For example, the four women here. Big sis Satsuki, big sis Mana, big sis Rina, and Hiromi-san. If they say they want to spend the night with me, I’d welcome with them open arms.」

「Oh my. That makes me happy.」

「Whoa, really? Yay!」

「Fweeeh.」

「Huh, huh?! M, me… too?」

Hearing Yuu’s words, each and every one of the women showed an amusing reaction.

Satsuki and Mana expressed their joy frankly, while Rina and Hiromi appeared to be more on the surprised side.

In particular, in Hiromi’s case, it might be because since she put her work above anything else, she had deliberately tried not to see Yuu as a man.

However, Yuu turned to Hiromi and nodded to show that he was serious and not joking.

As expected, Hiromi, who usually carried herself as a calm and mature woman, was shaken, becoming bright red in the face and turning her face down.

「Ahaha, that’s amazing. Then, I guess I can be at ease. But be careful not to push yourself too much and end up drained the next day.」

「Ah, yes. I’ll keep that in mind.」

And so the hour-long talk came to an end.

「Now then, once you’ve put your things down, I’ll show you around Hesperis from top to bottom.」

「Then, see you later.」

「Please enjoy yourself to your heart’s content.」

Unfortunately for Yuu, Hiromi said that she had some business to attend to in the board room.

Masaki also had plans to keep company some female guest members, so they went their separate ways.

The trio of Yuu, Mana, and Rina followed Satsuki, who led the way, and left the room.

+++

## **177 - Hot Spring Resort of Dreams! (3) ~Sisters~**

Following Satsuki, Yuu and the others took the elevator down to the fourth underground floor.

It seemed that this was the floor used for accommodation.

Looking at the floor plan, there were 10 Western-style rooms and 10 Japanese-style rooms split to the left and right, and apparently, at the back of the Western-style room side there was one particularly large room marked as a special room.

「Now, this way.」

Yuu was curious about what kind of room the special room was, but for now, he followed Satsuki down the hallway.

So far, they hadn’t encountered any other users, and the area was deserted and quiet.

It seemed to be a rule that the Western-style rooms were for both men and women, while the Japanese-style rooms were for women only, and room 10, which Yuu and the others entered, was a Western-style room of about 10 tatami mats.

In return for not having any window, hanging on the back wall was a huge painting depicting the scenery of Hakone with Lake Ashi at the center.

What caught his eye was the set of a double-sized bed and a sofa arranged facing each other.

I’d say it’s more like a love hotel.

While Yuu was having these impressions, Satsuki looked meaningfully at the three of them and said with a smile.

「Then, Yuu, Mana, Rina, are you okay with sharing a room with each other~?」

「Yeah, I don’t mind… Or rather, are big sis Mana and bis sis Rina okay with that?」

「I’d be happy to! Right, Rina?」

「Ah, yeah, err… if big sis says so…」

「Alright, it’s decided then! Now then, for now, put your luggage in the corner. Just in case, keep your valuables on you. I’ll keep the room key for you, so I’ll give it to you later. Let’s get going when you’re ready.」

「「Yes!」」

「Y… yes.」

Having their partners for the night decided to their liking, Yuu and Mana were in good spirits, while Rina alone replied with a flustered look on her face.

---

Yuu and the others, now lighter, went back to the elevator and went up to the above ground.

The interior, which was white with an image of blue sky and green plants, was refreshing and kind of reminded them of a sports facility.

「Ah, Satsuki-san! Hello!」

「Hello…huh?!」

「Oh my, hello.」

As they were walking down the aisle, they met two women in their mid-twenties.

I wonder if they are also my half-elder sisters; Yuu thought. Both of them were wearing light clothing, tank tops and shorts of different colors, and had towels draped over their shoulders. He could see that the ends of their hair, which were both tied up into a single bundle, were wet.

What was more, both of them were tall and had great figures, so Yuu couldn’t help but stare at them.

That being said, when they noticed Yuu, the two women were also surprised and stared at him with apparent curiosity, though.

「I’ve never seen them before.」

「Introduce them!」

「These two are here for the first time, so I’ve just started showing them around. It would take forever to tell each and every one of you one by one, so I’ll introduce them at dinner.」

「I see. Got it.」

「Yeah. I’m looking forward to it! See you later!」

After waving their hands with radiant smiles on their faces, both of them went in the direction Yuu and the others came from.

After that, they met a few more people and exchanged brief greetings with them, but Yuu noticed that there were differences in their tendencies.

Those who were acquainted not only with Satsuki but also with Mana were probably his half-elder sisters.

All of them were curious about Yuu and Rina, who they were seeing for the first time, but there was a clear sense of camaraderie and intimacy in their expressions.

And then, when Satsuki told them that she would introduce them at dinner, they readily left.

In contrast, the women who were barely acquainted with Satsuki or Mana, who they were meeting for the first time, stared only at Yuu intently with eyes that seemed to be sizing him up.

Even when Satsuki told them that she would introduce them at dinner, they were reluctant to leave.

According to Satsuki and Mana, they were probably guest members who had made it through the steep applicant-to-acceptance ratio.

As they had no idea when they would be able to come there again, they tended to get obsessed with the men they met.

Incidentally, the color of the nameplates of regular members, like Satsuki and Mana, and Yuu and Rina, who had just received theirs, was white.

The ones the women, who appeared to be guest members, that they met just a moment ago had were light blue, so with that, they should be able to easily tell them apart.

「Just in case, we’ll also keep an eye on them, but let us know if you find them too much. Ah, there are plain-clothed security guards with yellow nameplates patrolling the area, so please call out to them if you’re in trouble.」

「Okay. I understand. Thank you.」

They were probably concerned about Yuu, a man who was visiting for the first time.

He gratefully accepted those feelings, and after walking further on, they opened the door in the middle of the floor.

Apparently, they were going to climb the spiral staircase from there.

「Ooh… amazing.」

「Wow… so pretty!」

Setting aside Mana, who had been there before, Yuu and Rina were fascinated by the unusual plants that spread out in 360 degrees outside the window.

Just to name a few whose names they knew, there were tall palm trees, cycads, bananas with still green fruit, and agaves with huge, long, thin, pointed leaves sprouting from the ground.

There were also numerous flowers of various colors, including bougainvillea, cymbidium, and mandevilla.

There were several ponds scattered here and there, and the plants with round leaves were probably water lilies.

There were also a variety of cacti, from big to small.

Countless plants were planted throughout the area.

The ceiling was dome-shaped, and strong sunlight poured in through the glass.

「On cooler days, we can go outside and take a stroll there, but…」

「At this time of the year, it’s like a steam bath. I can’t stay there for more than five minutes.」

Hearing the conversation between Satsuki and Mana, Yuu was convinced.

The temperature inside the facility was kept at a comfortable level.

However, as soon as they climbed the spiral staircase and arrived here, he felt the temperature rise.

Furthermore, when he tried to touch the glass in front of him, he could feel the heat coming through it.

「Ah, so that’s the case.」

「Hmm?」

「Look, the plants that are planted here are all tropical ones, right? Moreover, the ceiling is made of glass, so it must be pretty hot and humid. In other words, this place is a tropical botanical garden.」

「I see. You sure know a lot, Yuu!」

「Nah, it’s nothing much. Ah, look. That cactus, it has a big flower in bloom.」

「Wow! You’re right. So it produces such beautiful flowers, huh.」

Mana smiled as she watched Yuu and Rina pointing here and there through the glass and talking naturally at such a close distance that shoulders were almost touching.

Without going out to the botanical garden, this time, they decided to go down the spiral staircase to listen to the explanation about the facilities on the first aboveground floor while actually touring them.

As soon as they opened the door, a smile naturally broke out on Yuu’s face.

After all, awaiting them there was a swimming pool, and he could see women in swimsuits enjoying themselves and making merry in it.

Though, compared to the size of the pool, the number of people using it seemed to be small, but as far as he could see, they were all women, which made him happy.

The high ceiling was made of transparent glass, radiating around the circle where the spiral staircase they had just climbed up and down was located.

There were windows, but not only were they high up, they were outward-facing windows that were only partially opened.

「This is the pool facility, which takes up about 3/4 of the first aboveground floor. There’s the so-called wave pool, where the waves come in like on a beach, a 25m pool like you’d find at a school, and a shallow pool for children and people who aren’t good at swimming.」

Right in front of Yuu and the others seemed to be the wave pool.

It was only about 100m wide and not very long, but the shore was the color of a sandy beach, and the water was shallow and the waves came in from the back.

From a distance, he could see that there were about 7 or 8 women in swimsuits, some were relaxing while holding onto floaties, and some others were having fun splashing water on each other.

As far as Yuu was concerned, he would have loved to watch them some more, but Satsuki and the others had moved on, so he couldn’t help but follow along.

For the 25m pool, unlike the ones that could be found at schools, it only had half the number of lanes, just 4.

This might be because those who used it were few in number.

In fact, there was only one person swimming there at the moment.

The crawl as they rotated their left and right arms alternately.

There was quite the distance between the place from where Yuu and the others were looking and the pool, but he could tell that they were swimming with excellent form.

They were wearing a swim cap and goggles, so he could see their face, but it looked like they also had a very good figure. So much that it made him think that they might be a real competitive swimmer.

Suddenly, when the person lifted their arm, Yuu saw something dark in their armpit, which surprised him inwardly.

At the very least, all the women he had mingled in the body with in this world had shaved their armpits, without exception.

「By any chance, is that person…」

「Oh my… I see he’s working hard today too.」

He found that surprising, and at the same time, he wondered if he could swim.

Before his rebirth, when he was young, he could swim as well as anyone else and would go to the pool or the sea to play.

However, at best, the Yuu of this world had only played in the water when he was in elementary school, and he had no memory of swimming in earnest.

Physical education classes were separated by gender from the fourth grade of elementary school, but swimming classes were optional for boys.

Therefore, boys who had entered puberty almost never swam.

They couldn’t go to places where they would be exposed to the eyes of women, such as the pool or the sea, so some of them might never swim throughout their lives.

That being said, even though he knew how to swim in his head, the question was whether he could swim physically.

Exercise was something you learned with your body, after all.

Since men couldn’t play outside as they pleased, having a place where they could move their bodies around like this was such a lifesaver.

The third underground floor was mainly an amusement center. To put it in a metaphor, you could say it was like a small-scale amusement facility.

「Doing it with fellow women is fine and all, but if possible, I’d like to have fun with a man, though.」

They gave their respective impressions as they returned to the stairs.

「I have to go help Ma-kun.」

Apparently, in exchange for being excluded from the housework groups, Satsuki and Masaki’s main task was to guide and explain things to members who were visiting for the first time, and to deal with various problems that might arise.

And that was a lot of work.

「Fufufu, you’re welcome. Well then, when it’s time for dinner, an announcement will be made throughout the facility, so until then, make yourself at home in your room.」

They were talking about the things they had seen in the facility until they entered the room, but as soon as they entered, they suddenly fell silent.

It might be because they couldn’t help but get conscious of the fact that they would be spending the night together, even though they had just met for the first time.

They opened their respective suitcase and organized their belongings, but perhaps feeling reserved around Yuu, the sisters spoke in low voices.

Similarly, Yuu was putting his clothes on hangers and putting out his toiletries, but all the while, he was lost in thought.

He ought to open up more with his two half-elder sisters, who he had been lucky enough to meet.

「Ah, I’ll…」

Rina’s face turned red.

「Ah… yes… Yuu, I love you.」

「Ahaha, you’re so cute, big sis Rina.」

When he kissed and hugged her again, Rina also timidly put her hands on Yuu’s shoulders and clung to him tightly.

「Hyan! How nice. I’m so jealous! Hey, Yuu… m, me too…」

「Hmm… sure. Big sis Mana, let’s have some kisses too.」

「Ahaan.」

This time, Yuu turned to Mana and looked at each other with her, and when she closed her eyes, he pressed his hips against hers and exchanged a passionate embrace with her.

For Mana, it wasn’t her first time doing it, but as soon as she had a kiss with Yuu, heat welled up in her chest and she felt like her mind was going to melt away, and before she knew it, she was actively exchanging kisses with him while calling out his name.

Then, Rina, who had gotten a taste of it, started to wish for it too, so he exchanged kisses with the two alternately over and over again.

For a while, he spent time making out with the two of them, and it seemed that time had passed.

An announcement was made throughout the facility, telling them that it was time for dinner.

## **178 - Hot Spring Resort of Dreams! (4) ~Men & Women~**

Perhaps the fact that Yuu had come had become widely known, it seemed that most of the regular and guest members had come to the dining hall.

Just as Yuu was about to go in there, hearing the commotion inside the dining hall that was audible even from the hallway, he was stopped by Satsuki and Masaki, so Mana and Rina alone went in first.

「We’d like to introduce you to our brothers who are here first, you see.」

「On a good day, close to 10 of them may gather here, but today, including you, there are only five of them, so it’s a bit lonely. Now, come over here.」

Getting called out by Satsuki, three men who appeared to be in their 20s who had been standing behind them stepped in front of Yuu.

He had a recollection of one of them.

Nearly 2 meters tall, he was a massive, sturdy and muscular man.

His chest, which was perceivable through his tank top, was thick, and his upper arms were as thick as the thighs of a slightly slender woman.

His hair was short, although not quite on the level of crew cut, and his skin was tanned to deep black color.

「Ahaha. Best regards.」

When Yuu shook the hand he held out to him, he not only had his hand gripped tightly, but also shaken up and down vigorously.

When it came to men of this world, he was a rare hot-blooded type, and all Yuu could do was reply to him with a wry smile.

「Good grief, you meathead… is that something to say to a little brother you’ve met for the first time? Ah, you don’t need to worry about that. For boys, studying is more important than such a thing, after all.」

「Study!」

「Geez, Kou-chan and Taku-chan always argues about that whenever they meet!」

After the elder brother who introduced himself as Kousaku, Yuu greeted the remaining two and shook hands with them.

「I’m Takuya. Best regards.」

「I’m Yuu. Nice to meet you.」

「I’ve always been the youngest, so I’m really happy to meet a little brother! I’m Tooru. Let’s get along.」

「Ahaha. Best regards, big bro Tooru.」

「Just Tooru is fine!」

「Whoa!」

The elder brother who introduced himself as Tooru didn’t just shake hands with him, but also hugged Yuu.

It would be understandable if it was between sisters, but he never thought he would come at him like that as brothers.

That was why Yuu, who was caught by surprise, ended up getting hugged tightly.

To his chagrin, a soft, girlish, nice scent tickled his nose, and even though they were both guys, it didn’t make him feel uncomfortable.

The eldest, Masaki, worked as a staff in the Toyota Sakuya Memorial Foundation.

Because of this, he traveled back and forth between Hesperis and the headquarters every week in August.

Takuya was 23 years old. He was a graduate student living in Kanagawa Prefecture. He was tall enough to be described as gangly, probably around 180cm. On top of that, he had unhealthily pale skin and wore silver-rimmed glasses, giving him a finicky impression, but he showed a friendly attitude towards Yuu.

He worked hard on his research every day, even during summer vacation, but apparently, after getting forcefully invited by Kousaku and the other brothers, he reluctantly came there.

The last one, Tooru, was 20 years old. He lived in Tokyo and attended a famous private university.

With his silky brown hair grown to his shoulders, he didn’t not look like a frivolous person, but his androgynous face reminded him of his high school friend Higashino Rei.

His most distinctive features were, as expected, his pigeon-toeing sissy-like mannerisms and girlish speech. He was almost like an okama.

For your sakes, I might even be willing to amend the laws of this country to allow marriage between siblings. As long as you remain allies of my nation, of course." 

"Both my sister and I intend to serve you for the rest of our lives."

I had no choice but to say that. Sis... why did you have to evolve in such a reckless way?! Think about me, having to follow up on this...!

"I think it’s a well-balanced evolution for a brother and sister!" 

"Lady Staff, what side are you on?!"

While we were talking, More and Bloom, super-charged by my sister’s skill, continued to indiscriminately crush the students involved in the commotion. It was already a chaotic situation where dividing them into "More for commoners" and "Bloom for nobles" didn't even matter anymore.

Sis also galloped her horse through the battlefield, tearing through it in every direction. It’s not like those were all the students in the school, and most of the strong ones had already advanced in the "One Day Heaven-Breaking Ceremony" and been crushed by me anyway. Still, she was having a great time dominating the field.

Technically, those two are second-year students, so most of the people they were beating up were their seniors.

"That’s just how incredible the reinforcement from the skill is. On top of that, there's still the room for the multiplicative reinforcement from your skill, so it’s far too terrifying."

**[Vow of the Carnal Feast]** x **[Sex Boost]**. I wonder what the maximum reinforcement multiplier would be?

"In the future, I might organize an elite all-female unit with you siblings as commanders. At any rate, the problem before us seems like it will be settled shortly." 

"By using the overly crude method of 'crushing everything,' though."

But what was the meaning of all this development up to now? This trouble that suddenly broke out after the end of the "One Day Heaven-Breaking Ceremony" felt like the flow was a bit too forced. The friction from my conflict with the former Suppapan Seminar was fanned into a riot? It felt like too much of a stretch.

"Why did this happen?" 

"It’s likely just a spiteful harassment from those who couldn't have things their way," the Queen smiled playfully. She had the look of someone who had won.

"Since Sao has been crushing every single one of their plots and schemes, they must have finally gotten impatient. It’s a very sudden and messy setup—this is exactly the kind of timing where you can catch them by the tail."

It was at that moment. Something thin and sharp flew toward the Queen.

It was moving at a speed the eye couldn't even follow.

"Look out!!"

Before I could even move to stop it, the needle, instead of piercing the Queen's beautiful skin, burst into flames in mid-air and was incinerated.

+++

### **73 - The Abandoned Princess's Desperation**

 "That just now... was it a blowgun?!"

I quickly deduced the identity of the thin needle that had come flying toward Her Majesty.

A blowgun—a long-range weapon that sends a small projectile flying through a tube with the force of a breath. Because they are small and easy to carry, they are perfect tools for assassination.

_To think someone would fire something like that at the Queen... Her Majesty almost got assassinated again?!_

However, the assassination failed before I even had time to be surprised. The needle heading for the Queen had spontaneously ignited.

_Was that the flames of **[Pyro Stigma]**?!_

I didn't do it... That's right, the Queen herself had met the Fire Spirit, Napalm, at the end of her own adventures long ago and had been engraved with a mark of affection. Having held it for decades, she surely wields it far more skillfully than a novice like me.

"...Ha?! An intruder! The Queen was targeted! Come out, come out, guards!"

"Do not act rashly, Sao. A toy like that couldn't take my life, let alone leave a scratch."

She was referring to the blowgun. It was indeed impressive how it burned to ash instantly. Once again, I was reminded: she isn't just a lewd older woman—she is the Queen.

"Hmm? I smell the scent of lèse-majesté..." 

"N-Never mind that! We have to catch the assassin!" 

"Quite right. Spear, Voulge, Estoc, Flammea."

The ones called were the noble ladies—the very ones who, until a moment ago, were drowning in a harem sex session.

"It is time for you lot to show your worth. Escort our 'guest' back to us. You are surely the most suitable for the task."

The wording was roundabout, but it clearly meant: "Go drag that assassin here."

"You are all under the influence of that female knight's skill. Your base abilities should be drastically increased. If you fail despite that, there is truly no point in the nobility existing. Do it as if your lives depend on it." 

"Y-Yes!" 

"Leave it to us!"

Spurred on by the Queen’s sharp words, Spear and the others sprinted off like a shot. Their movements were incomparably faster than when they had fought me. They were being buffeted by my sister's skill, 《Vow of the Dallying Feast》. Since they were all girls who had just had their virginity taken by me, the effect was instantaneous.

"A blowgun... To target me with a mere concealed weapon that carries neither skill nor magic—don't you think that is proof they are finally cornered, Sao?" 

"Huh?" I tilted my head, not following the Queen’s intent.

"Goodness, you're unexpectedly slow. Weren't you the one who said this commotion was too forced and unnatural? This lacks the meticulousness of the time they used Lespar to send assassins all the way into my bedroom."

If this entire sequence—from fanning the flames of student conflict to the chaos—was a singular move to get a shot at the Queen...

"When cornered, one becomes dull. They tried to confuse the succession by deceiving Lespar, but that was swiftly settled once I became pregnant. Their plan to exhaust our nation by inciting conflict between nobles and commoners is now hollow as well. Though, all of that was resolved by Sao."

"...So there’s a villain trying to harm this country, operating in the shadows. Their plans kept failing, and they started to panic?"

"You're getting sharper, Sao. For them, today was the ultimate opportunity. Eliminating me is the best move to strike a blow against this country. After all, I _am_ a wise and virtuous ruler."

_...She really just says it herself, doesn't she?_

"If they missed today, I would return to the castle, making it far more difficult to target me. They rushed to seize a sliver of a chance, but that haste will be their undoing. Sloppy plans ultimately ruin everything—including one's own safety."

Before long, Spear returned to report that they had captured the culprit. The criminal was an unexpected person.

---

"I am terribly sorry!!"

Spear pressed her forehead against the ground in apology. Even though she had successfully captured the assassin as ordered, the identity of the culprit was the problem.

"She is..."

I recognized the woman bound in ropes.

"The one who audaciously targeted Her Majesty’s life... was the attendant I brought with me! As her master, I must bear the blame as well! I wish to atone for this crime with my life!!"

 "I have no need for your life, you fool."

Ignoring Spear’s tragic plea, the Queen simply walked toward the young assassin.

"Well, I had a general idea. The discriminatory ideology between nobles and commoners that eats away at the country... I wondered who brought such a divisive way of thinking into the Royal School, the heart of human resource development..." 

"..."

I had met Spear’s attendant before. When we first met, I thought she was such a good-natured woman that my heart fluttered. To think such a gentle-looking person would target the Queen... terrifying.

"Suppapan was merely a container, wasn't he? He was also on the side that was deceived. He didn't have the capacity to be the deceiver. Someone used his title and power to create a box to fill with poisonous ideology. That was the 'Suppapan's Seminar,' I assume?" 

"..." The girl said nothing.

"The role of pouring poison into the prepared box was yours. Commoner students enter the school under the guise of being guards for noble children. You took advantage of that custom to infiltrate noble houses with young sons and daughters. No one would ever suspect a commoner was the one spreading the 'discriminate against commoners' ideology, would they?"

As the Queen chuckled, Spear’s face grew even paler. It made sense; her own inner circle had plotted the assassination of the monarch.

"A-Um, Your Majesty...?"

"Do not worry. I am well aware that you were also deceived. Though, I am disappointed that a noble who is meant to carry the country was so easily misled."

By the way, it wasn't just the young attendant bound at our feet. Two others were rolled up in ropes nearby.

"This person attended this school as the attendant of the son of Viscount Junirius, who graduated last year. He should have graduated as well." 

"This one is the attendant of Kodra, a current third-year student..."

Both were commoner students who had entered the school through the same channels as Sis and I. One had even already graduated. They entered to follow their masters. And those masters...

"Were they members of the Suppapan's Seminar?"

At the Queen's guess, those around her nodded.

"So you've been sending spies continuously. By doing so, you intended to spread discriminatory ideology within the school without end, eventually fanning the conflict between commoners and nobles across the entire nation. An ambitious... no, a truly patient plot."

"I have brought the records." The school administration was likely the most shaken by this. One of the teachers, who had worked hard to help with the capture and settle the chaos, held out a document.

"These are the records of the 'Rite of Heavenly Decree' for all students. This graduate's 'Divine Calling' is [Agitator], and this current third-year's Divine 'Calling' is [Illusionist]...!"

"Classes perfectly suited for confusing people and inviting them to their deaths. Did the school have no warning about students with such dangerous 'Divine Calling'?" 

"W-We are terribly sorry...! In daily classes, they didn't stand out at all, so we didn't think they were capable of much...!"

_Agitation_—to fan the flames of people’s hearts and direct them toward an intended action. 

_Illusion_—likely a 'Divine Calling' with magic-based skills for showing illusions. One could surmise both were classes skilled in manipulating the human mind.

"So the unnatural conflict that almost broke out between students just now was also...?!" 

"It must have been their doing. Using the **[Agitation]** skill to fan the ill feelings of an unspecified number of people, and the **[Illusionist]**'s skills to dull their judgment and push them toward a riot."

And the fact that the Suppapan's Seminar students became such stubborn bigots was likely due to their skills playing a part in the brainwashing.

"Who on earth are they?" I asked, unable to contain myself. 

"To infiltrate unnoticed and spread discord, making people hate each other and rotting a group from the inside...! This is exactly like spy sabotage! What do they gain from doing this?!"

"Not 'exactly like'—it _is_ sabotage." 

"Is it that Neo-Assassin Guild group that was mentioned before?!" 

"No, they are far bigger than those punks. Hey, you lot. You may think you're hiding your identities well, but I have a good idea who you are."

At the Queen's statement, the three captives widened their eyes.

"Only another nation could attempt to tear down a giant like a country, right? A nation of a scale large enough to pick a fight with a Great Power ruled by a wise monarch like myself. The one likely to take such underhanded measures to chip away at our foundations from the shadows... is the 'Land of Tigers and Wolves' to the west, **Niosebuk**."

Struck by the truth, the prisoners trembled even more.

"Kill me!"

Suddenly, the girl who had been silent until now—the one posing as Spear’s attendant—barked out. She began to scream with a fire that made her previous silence feel like a lie.

"What a vivid reaction. You might as well be confessing that I hit the bullseye." 

"Shut up! You whore, you profligate Queen of Renisegura! If I am to be captured by the likes of you, I would proudly choose death! Kill me! Kill me quickly!"

The intensity of her transformation was so strong it shocked even her supposed master. In contrast, the Queen didn't bat an eye even when showered with such raw hatred. That’s our Queen!

"The Great Western Power, Niosebuk, is a brutal land commonly known as the 'Land of Tigers and Wolves.' It is a nest of madmen who are constantly at war, whether through internal strife or foreign conquest." 

"Huh...?!" I listened as the Queen started explaining with total composure, ignoring the girl's madness.

"They attack and annex neighboring countries, force princesses of royal blood into marriage to bear their children... I hear the current King of Niosebuk has about fifty princes and princesses. If you include unrecognized illegitimate children, it probably exceeds a hundred." 

"What a scumbag!"

"Even so, his desire for conquest is not satisfied, and now he has targeted my great nation. No, seeing how they've come at us with such meticulous, underhanded tactics, the invasion itself must have been decided long ago..." The Queen shook her head with a sigh.

"Even though they were cleverly hidden, it was a lapse on my part not to notice until now. To think even succession candidates like Lespar and Suppapan were seduced... I have to admit, I've been played." 

"But those cowardly attacks ended in failure." 

"That is entirely the result of Sao's efforts. Driving away the shadows that cling to our nation... Truly, Sao is the guardian of our country!"

When the Queen said that, the captured girl glared at me with sharp, piercing eyes. It was as if she were saying, "So it's your fault we failed?!"

"So these people are spies from the Kingdom of Niosebuk?" 

"Well... I wonder about that?"

_Eh? You're making that uncertain now?!_

"Don't be in such a rush. There is no doubt they were sent from Niosebuk. But, you know, what we've caught might be a 'big fish' too large to even be called a 'spy'."

"?"

As I was confused, a figure in black clothes suddenly appeared before us as if emerging from the shadows. A ninja?! It was a ninja!

"Good work," the Queen said. The ninja handed some documents to the Queen and disappeared instantly.

"Underhanded work isn't the exclusive specialty of your country, you know? Let’s see... ah, here it is. Seeker, the 19th Princess of Niosebuk. That is your true identity, isn't it?"

Everyone present couldn't believe their ears. The captured girl bit her lip, trying to endure. The most shocked of all was likely Spear, who had been her master.

"P-Please wait, Your Majesty... Not only was my attendant a spy for another country... but a Princess? There must be some mistake."

"Normally, one would think so. It's impossible for a princess to be sent as a spy. Unless it's that 'Land of Tigers and Wolves'." The Queen spoke with a sigh.

"In that country, birth status means nothing. The only thing that speaks is ability. More specifically, the performance of the 'Divine Calling' one is born with. If you are born with a good 'Divine Calling', even an orphan can rise to greatness; if not, even royalty is cast aside. That is that kind of country."

The Queen explained that this was why it was called the "Land of Tigers and Wolves." A merit-based society where only ability matters—a policy unique to a warmongering state that has continuously engaged in invasion.

"Because it is that kind of nation, they can use underhanded tactics like dividing the noble and commoner classes in other countries. In their country, which is merit-based and thinks nothing of status, class discrimination could never occur. Revenge in kind is impossible." 

"I see..."

"It seems this princess was not blessed with a very good 'Divine Calling', either. Well, depending on how you use it, it’s quite a terrifying 'Divine Calling'. Perhaps that’s why she was made into a spy."

Even a princess is forced to be a spy based on her 'Divine Calling' aptitude. That is the merit-based 'Land of Tigers and Wolves'...?!

"...That’s right! My ability is not fit for a ruler! That’s why I’m forced into the role of a shadow-dwelling spy! In my country, only those with true power can call themselves royalty! Only those born with the 'Divine Calling' of a Ruler, like the Third Prince or the Eighth Princess!"

In a state of near-desperation, she began to scream.

"Compared to that, your country is so carefree! It’s a joke that you can act grand based only on where you were born, regardless of ability! Incompetents who aren't even strong act grand just because they're 'nobles'! I had a hard time holding back my laughter watching that! It is the right future for a spineless country like this to be ruled by our Niosebuk Kingdom!!"

"Are those sour grapes? Will you be satisfied if you scream that much?" The Queen’s eyes glowed coldly. No monarch remains calm when their country is insulted.

"Tigers and wolves have no room for familial affection. That is why your nation is called the 'Land of Tigers and Wolves.' Someone from such a country has become a prisoner of another nation. You understand what that means, don't you?"

"I understand perfectly. Even if I am a princess, I have no value as a hostage. Because I’m an incompetent with no great 'Divine Calling'. Just kill me already."

Her defiance seemed like she had made peace with her fate, but at the same time, she looked completely self-destructive.

"Wait a minute."

If this continued, she really would be executed. I spoke up to stop that flow. I recalled the ninja's report that had briefly entered my field of vision...

"Could you leave her disposal to me? I have an idea."

### **74 - The Archenemy Appears**

The Kingdom of Niosebuk.

Located at the western edge of the world, it was a mighty nation boasting top-tier territory and national power.

Its operations were fueled by a thorough meritocracy; treatment was determined by achievements and abilities, regardless of birth status, race, or skin color. If you had the ability, even an orphan could rise to greatness; if you lacked it, even a prince would be cast aside.

The legions that survived this harsh selection were elites. Once they set upon a neighboring country, they would crush the enemy army, burn villages and towns to the ground, march straight to the royal castle, and behead the king and princes. Then, young queens and princesses were taken back to the motherland as spoils of war. In fact, regardless of status, every healthy woman judged capable of bearing strong children was taken. Everyone else was slaughtered.

It is said that the number of annexed vassal states has reached ten. "Vassal state" was a name in title only; once ruled, the history and culture fostered there until then were utterly destroyed, leaving no trace behind.

Might is right. It was the way of the Niosebuk Kingdom to thoroughly force this ideology upon the enemies they defeated.

The current head of this villainous kingdom, King Imashinunda I, was celebrating his 47th birthday today. A nationwide celebratory ceremony was held, and in the capital of the Niosebuk Kingdom... the Royal Capital, Ganinva, the city was packed with domestic dignitaries, princes and princesses granted succession rights, and palace warriors who had achieved great deeds and garnered respect and awe. Alongside them were the "wives" they had taken—slave women who bore the title of wife but carried only the duty of birthing children.

Tens of thousands of residents living in the capital crowded into the Royal Castle Square.

Appearing on a balcony built at a particularly high vantage point was a man radiating a cold, domineering aura. This man was the leader of the "Land of Tigers and Wolves," King Imashinunda I of Niosebuk.

Having reached his 47th birthday and nearing his fifties, his body remained sturdy, covered in muscles that looked like bundles of wire. His slender yet thoroughly trained frame was like a sharp, famous sword, and his gaze was equally, if not more, piercing.

When the King appeared in public, the crowd fell silent for a moment to catch their breath, then erupted into cheers of praise for the sovereign.

"Our King, the strongest!" 

"There is no king in heaven or earth more brilliant than His Majesty Imashinunda!" 

"The one fit to rule the world!"

Those shouts of praise were born more from the fear that they would be killed if they didn't say them. The King found more satisfaction in the fear underlying the words than in the praise itself...

"The weak must die; they serve no purpose even if they live."

The speech began.

"That is the providence of our country. We have attacked and destroyed many nations, and beheaded the losers. I believe the prosperity of our country is solely proof that this providence is correct."

The King of Niosebuk continued.

"Strength is justice. The strong can have everything. That is the most absolute and simple law of this world. Turning one's eyes away from that and mixing in trivial elements to make the world cluttered is nothing more than the weak escaping from reality."

"Exactly!" 

"Love and hearts are just the nonsense of the weak!" voices rose from the guest seats. It was proof that the entire nation was subservient to that mad King.

"That is why I will continue to fight. Until this world is covered by the law of strength. Today, I have reached my 47th birthday. But neither my heart nor my body has withered. I promise to continue expanding the flames of war with all my might and give our citizens the chance for prosperity and advancement."

An "Ooooooh!" of echoing cheers arose.

"The next target has already been decided. The great eastern nation, the Kingdom of Renisegura! A weakling state that gluttonously devours indolence in peace without striving in war! I shall burn that country to the ground with the fires of war, and take the Queen—said to be noble and beautiful—as my 17th wife! The weak are ruled by the strong! That is the absolute providence!"

The entire venue boiled over at the King's new declaration of war.

It was war. By destroying, pillaging, and seizing, further prosperity could be hoped for. Such vulgar expectations seethed in the eyes of everyone, subjects and commoners alike.

"Prepare for war! Let your hearts seethe and awaken the beast within you! We, the Kingdom of Niosebuk, are the 'Land of Tigers and Wolves'! It is said to be the land where tigers and wolves live! What a glorious name! Both tigers and wolves are the strong among beasts! Kill and devour every last one of those dull domestic animals!"

The King of Niosebuk was at the height of his pride on his own birthday.

"I am the master of the strongest tigers and wolves, King Imashinunda I of Niosebuk! My legend is still in the making! Eventually, I shall rule this entire world and impregnate every woman in this world with my seed! My name alone shall be the title of a legend that lasts for thousands and tens of thousands of years! Guhahahahahaha!!"

Right in the middle of his peak of triumph...

_THOOM!_

A massive hole opened up in his torso.

"Wh...?"

Not just the King himself, but every single royal, subordinate, and citizen attending the King's birthday ceremony who was focused on him was lost for words in shock. As if the cheers from a moment ago were a lie, all sound vanished. Everyone forgot even to scream, staring at the hole that had opened in the King's abdomen.

"Eh? Ah? This is...?!"

It was a hole larger than a fist, roughly the diameter of a handball. Anyone could tell that if such a hole opened in one's gut, it was a certain fatal wound. The King of the "Land of Tigers and Wolves" was dying on his auspicious birthday.

"...Why am I... dying?"

Immediately after those words—too pathetic to be a last testament—his head shattered into pieces, scattering bits of flesh like crushed tomatoes in every direction.

---

"Right, mission accomplished."

The archenemy appeared and died instantly.

It's me. It’s Sao, the protagonist of this story.

Well, in this world where everyone lives with their own wishes, everyone is a protagonist. Except for the scumbags who take away those people's wishes and futures and act like it's only natural.

"Really... Did we really just assassinate the King of Niosebuk...?" 

"Told you, didn't I? We could do it if you cooperated."

Beside me was Lady Seeker, the princess of the Niosebuk Kingdom who had been sent to our country as a spy. The reason I forcibly brought her back on a "homecoming" was because her 'Divine Calling' was necessary for the assassination of the Niosebuk King.

Her 'Divine Calling' is **[Voyeur]**. You might wonder, "Is that even a 'Diving Calling'?" but the more you hear about its abilities, the more terrifying they are. Her held skills start with **[Long-Range Vision]** ; fitting for a **[Voyeur]**, she can accurately and clearly see things from a distance as if using a telescope. She also possesses many high-performance skills perfect for covert activities, such as **[X-ray Vision]** and **[Presence Concealment]**.

It makes sense to deploy such talent as a scout, but it’s a mystery why they treated her so poorly despite her being so gifted in espionage. If it were me, I’d use her as much as Ethan Hunt. Is that country stupid?

"In this country, only 'Divine Calling' specialized in direct combat are considered superior. Espionage is looked down upon as something cowards do. That’s why I, who had an aptitude for it, was immediately stripped of my succession rights and forced to become a spy."

They told her, _"Because you only have that much value,"_ and _"We'll keep you alive only as long as you're recognized as having value, so work hard."_

"Those were the only words my father... no, the King, ever said to me. He has no familial affection. He’s a monster who decides everything based solely on whether someone is useful to him!" 

"Oh... wow." 

"And now I've had a hand in that man's assassination! Serves him right! The skill he threw away as useless helped kill him! There's no story more refreshing than this! You idiot, thinking I'd be sad! Did you think I'd cry over my father's death?! Why on earth would I have a reason to cry for a scumbag like that!"

Princess Seeker was cheering rather than crying over the death of the King. I had felt quite hesitant about the inhuman act of making her help assassinate her own father, but it was a needless worry.

Anyway, the point is that I assassinated the King of Niosebuk.

Let me explain how I did it. First, relying on Princess Seeker's 《Long-Range Vision》 skill, we climbed the bell tower of a church located about 5km away from the Niosebuk Royal Castle where the ceremony was being held. From that high vantage point, we could look around without any obstructions, and we could clearly see the balcony of the castle where the King of Tigers and Wolves stood.

It was incredibly far, though.

Princess Seeker’s **[Long-Range Vision]** solved that; even from far away, I could see him as if he were within arm's reach. Being at such a long distance also ensured our own safety—two birds with one stone.

Still, you’re probably thinking, _“Seeker is the one with the skill, it has nothing to do with you.”_ That’s where I used a new skill of my own.

It's a skill called **[Shared Property]**, which allows me to treat the target's held skills as my own temporarily. The condition? Having sex.

While my male organ is inserted into a specific female organ, I can freely use one of that woman's skills. Well, since we’re having sex, the skills I can realistically use are limited by the posture.

Princess Seeker’s skill cleared the conditions. So, currently, I had pulled her skirt up and inserted from behind, and in that state, I used **[Long-Range Vision]** to snipe the King of Niosebuk.

My **[Extend]** skill has reached a high level of performance through leveling up, so I can instantly extend the pole I’m holding 5km away and instantly pull it back. The whole sequence took less than a hundredth of a second.

There were tens of thousands of people packed into the ceremony, but I’m sure no one noticed the moment it extended, let alone the moment it retracted. All they could notice was the result: the pole, extended with speed exceeding the speed of sound, pierced through that crappy King's gut, opening a massive hole. And the second shot that blew his head off.

The movement was exactly like sniping. I felt like Golgo 13.

"It’s amazing. To combine various skills and come up with an assassination method like this. No one will ever notice that the King was killed from such a distant place."

As if to prove that...

Soldiers swarmed into the venue of the King's birthday ceremony, blockading the area to prevent the crowd from leaving. They likely judged that the assassin was hiding among that mass of people. That’s the common-sense conclusion. But the culprit wasn't in there!

"Whoa, the people are starting to revolt! Whoa, they punched a soldier!" 

"It’s the 'Land of Tigers and Wolves,' so even the commoners are hot-blooded. A brawl is inevitable now. I wonder how many hundreds of deaths will come from that alone..."

The "Land of Tigers and Wolves" is scary.

"But will this avoid war?"

The reason I assassinated a foreign king like this was, of course, because I wanted to avoid a war starting in the country where I live. A cruel neighbor is targeting our home. I'd rather kill a foreign king without hesitation than have the people and land I love harmed or defiled. To protect what I love. And if that king is a demonic scoundrel, I have even less hesitation.

"But even if the King dies, the country remains, right?"

What if the Tiger and Wolf nation doesn't discard its war policy after the King's death and comes to attack our country led by a new leader...?

"There’s no need to worry about that. From now on, this country will enter a long state of civil war. For sure."

"Ehh?" 

"While you're ravishing me, you can use my 《Long-Range Vision》, right? Look at the group standing to the right of the King's body." 

"To the right?"

I stared at the right side of the castle balcony as Seeker told me. There, about ten young men and women were lined up. Everyone was confused and shocked by the sudden disaster... but in their expressions, there was a trace of giddy joy. Like, "The path to my glory has opened!"?

"Of course. The only ones who can sit in the royal family seats there are the King's children... and moreover, the powerful ones who haven't had their succession rights stripped yet." 

"The children of the King I just killed? ...Alright, maybe I should shoot them dead, too..." 

"Stop it. Those ones are more useful alive," Seeker said. What did she mean?

"The fact that the current King died means the next King will be chosen from among those people. Furthermore, this country is a total meritocracy. Regardless of order or formality, the truly strong prince or princess will succeed their father. ...What do you think will happen?"

Who is stronger and superior? There is only one way to decide that...

"So, a civil war..." 

"From now on, the Niosebuk Kingdom will begin a bloody civil war over the new throne. It’ll be no time for invading other countries. This land will be devastated by the fruitless struggles of my idiot brothers and sisters who are conceited enough to think they're 'the strongest.' Isn't that what you want, too?"

I guess so. The longer the civil war lasts, the longer the damage to my country is postponed. I have no choice but to hope they kill each other as much as they want.

"In fact, from your perspective, the appropriate response would be to pull strings behind the scenes so the civil war lasts as long as possible. Supporting the disadvantaged side of the conflict. Fanning the flames by spreading ominous rumors..."

While the wolves devour each other, the peace of humans is maintained. That’s fine, but...

"Why are you being so helpful?" 

"Eh?"

To play along with the diversion, Big Sis Calibaur and the rest of the women had all left the inn to hunt goblins. So, the only ones moving energetically here were me and the enemy goblins, but...

"A goblin is talking?"

Is that possible? To speak means it understands human language. However, the figure that emerged through the ranks of the general goblins was far too tall and slender for a goblin, with a dignified posture.

"What is it? Is it so rare for a goblin to speak?" 

"Pardon my ignorance, but I’ve never heard of a goblin that could use human speech."

But is that thing really a goblin? Its build—its skeletal structure—was clearly fashion-model grade.

"I am no ordinary goblin. I am a special goblin who has survived the struggle for existence, lived long, and evolved accordingly. Do not lump me in with those common types."

As I thought. A mutated goblin. Even the "Rokuburin" (Level 6) I saw back in the countryside possessed enough cunning to change the course of a battle.

Since that day, I had set it in my mind: if a Goblin becomes a Rokuburin, then surely a Nanaburin or Hachiburin (Level 7 or 8) would appear, and the day would come when I’d face them.

Today, that time finally came. My heart was ready; I wouldn't be surprised no matter how many "-burin" it was. Bring it on.

"I am the highest-ranking goblin who has stepped into the end of ultimate evolution! Having achieved a 10,005-stage evolution, my name is...!"

He paused for effect.

"...The Man-Goblin!!" 

"That's too many stages!?"

Even for me, the number of evolution stages far exceeded my expectations. He passed ten thousand!?

"Fuhfuhfuh, you seem surprised. From the perspective of I, a Man-Goblin, humans are nothing but inferior organisms! Savor your one-sided terror!!" 

"Shut up, you just sound like a Mango Pudding!" 

"Keep acting tough while you can. My strategy is slowly cornering you. How many dozens of my kin have you crushed? Even if each one is trash, you consume a tiny bit of power to strike them. As that piles up, you will certainly reach the peak of exhaustion."

This guy is using his comrades as pawns just to drain my stamina? And not just one, but dozens? I felt disgust at his cruel strategy, but at the same time, I was impressed by this "Man-Goblin's" command ability—forcing self-centered goblins, who don't have a shred of devotion, to carry out suicide charges. He’s making goblins—who would gladly sacrifice their parents or children to survive—perform sacrificial acts. I could finally accept the absurdity of a 10,000-stage evolution.

"If I defeat you, the barrier behind you will vanish, won't it? Then we can enter that big house and take whatever we want, killing every human inside!"

Actually, someone else cast that holy barrier, so my safety doesn't matter. More importantly, the premise that I’d be beaten by you guys is impossible.

"It’s true that moving my body makes me tired. But the absolute amount of stamina differs from person to person." 

"What?"

With one swing of my pole, nearly ten trash goblins were swept away.

"Wha—!? Even after fighting this much, your movements are still sharp!?" 

"If you want to make me run out of stamina, you’d better bring ten thousand goblins."

I haven't spent day and night having sex with over ten lovers for nothing. Endurance is my greatest specialty.

"But I hate wasting time, so let’s finish this quickly."

I simply hated spending the time. I pulled out another pole, one for my right hand and one for my left. Dual-polr style. With this, I could eradicate the goblins at twice the speed. Crossing the two poles into a cross shape, I emitted an energy-like force, releasing something like a wave motion cannon!

"Haaaaaaaaaa!!"

With that, most of the goblins were blown away and evaporated. When you master the **[Pole Master]** skills, you can do things like this.

"Hieeeeee!? What is this human!? Hieeeeeee!?"

In the midst of that, the one called Man-Goblin stubbornly survived. As expected of an ultimately evolved goblin. His reactions were overwhelmingly faster than the others, and he was sturdy to boot.

"I can't deal with a monster like that! I'm leaving!"

As soon as he realized he was at a disadvantage, his speed in fleeing was exactly like a goblin. But I couldn't let him go. If a goblin that far evolved was released back into the world, he would surely build a massive horde again and become a plague to human society. To prevent the damage from repeating, I had to cut the root of the trouble here. I’d already made arrangements.

"Where do you think you're going, Mr. Goblin? From here, it’s a direct course to hell." 

"You won't escape."

Big Sis Calibur and Lady Staff appeared. They stood in the path of the retreating Man-Goblin, cutting off his escape.

"You guys!? Where did you come from!?" 

"We're the ones who went to exterminate the diversionary goblins you prepared. Though, we annihilated them long ago and came back like this."

Seeing a high possibility of a mutated goblin being on the enemy side, we had prepared and coordinated from the start. My sister and the others wiped out the diversionary goblins at maximum speed, then turned back to set up an encirclement around the hot spring inn. If the goblins were going to be sneaky, they’d strike the inn, so the plan was for me to intercept them and stall the front line while they prepared a formation to let not a single one slip through.

The plan worked perfectly. The fleeing goblins were surely being picked off by Spear, Bloom, and the others. Being able to set up such a flawless formation so quickly was an ability unique to my **[Holy Knight]** sister.

"Only the boss left, it seems." 

"So this is the mutated goblin I've heard rumors about. They say if even one joins a pack, a pest cull turns into a war. We certainly can't let this go."

Neither Big Sis Calibur nor Lady Staff had any intention of forgiving this evil evolved being. Shall we swing the blade of judgment to conclude the battle? It's a pole, though.

"W-w-w-wait, wait! Is it okay to kill me just like this!? I still have a trump card!"

That’s the kind of ugly struggle unique to a goblin. So what if you have a trump card? If you do, stop the tedious talk and counterattack with it right now.

"Fuhfuhfuh... You still don't understand, do you? I am the ultimate mutated species, Man-Goblin, who has achieved 10,005 stages of evolution...! Behold the special organ possessed only by a Man-Goblin!"

What!?

"Only in a Man-Goblin... yes, it is a goblin with a pussy (Oman-ko)!!" 

"A dirty joke!?"

The sheer stupidity of it made me land a single middle-finger fist right on the Man-Goblin's crown. A pun? And a dirty one? Pulling a combo of things you shouldn't do just made me feel even sadder.

"But what was that goblin trying to do by showing its pussy?" 

"A honey trap, maybe?"

Regardless, we defeated the final goblin general. Quest complete! We wiped out the goblins while protecting the hot spring inn!!

---

"Thank you so much!!"

After the post-battle cleanup, the landlady of the inn expressed her intense gratitude. To ensure the goblin corpses wouldn't attract other vicious monsters or cause disease, we burned them thoroughly and buried them deep in the ground.

Before that, we cut off their ears, sealed them in a bucket, and sent them via "cool delivery" to the Lord ruling this area. As proof that the goblins were handled. I included a letter saying, "Don't make passersby do your job for you; I'll be sure to report this to the Queen," so his future handling of things shouldn't be too bad.

"I'm sure the business suspension will be revoked immediately. This is all thanks to you. I really can't thank you enough!"

"No, no, we just did what humans ought to do based on duty and compassion. Besides, we want to fulfill our original purpose for coming to this inn."

"Of course! I won't hesitate to reward the benefactors who saved my inn. Please, heal the fatigue of battle in our waters! Since we're officially closed, there are no other guests! You can have the place all to yourselves!"

All to ourselves!? Hyahoi! Having a whole hot spring inn to ourselves—what a wonderful situation!

Since that’s the case, there’s only one thing to do! Let’s get in the spring!!

+++
